Interface Definition\n**File:** `internal/storage/storage.go`\n\nUpdated the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface to include:\n```go\nFlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)\n```\n\nThis method provides a lightweight way to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object.\n\n### 2. SQL Store Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/sql/common/flag.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the SQL Store:\n- Uses a SQL query with `COUNT(*) > 0` to efficiently check existence\n- Respects the namespace and key from the ResourceRequest\n- Returns `(true, nil)` if the flag exists, `(false, nil)` otherwise\n- Returns `(false, err)` on database errors\n\n```go\nfunc (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {\n    var exists bool\n    err := s.builder.Select(\"COUNT(*) > 0\").\n        From(\"flags\").\n        Where(sq.Eq{\"namespace_key\": p.Namespace(), \"\\\"key\\\"\": p.Key}).\n        QueryRowContext(ctx).\n        Scan(&exists)\n    if err != nil {\n        return false, err\n    }\n    return exists, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Filesystem Snapshot Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/fs/snapshot_flag_exists.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the Snapshot type:\n- Checks if the flag exists in the in-memory namespace map\n- Returns `(false, nil)` if the namespace doesn't exist (not an error)\n- Returns `(true, nil)` if the flag exists in the namespace\n- Returns `(false, nil)` if the flag doesn't exist\n\n```go\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {\n    ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n    if err != nil {\n        return false, nil\n    }\n    _, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]\n    return ok, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Filesystem Store Wrapper Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/fs/store_flag_exists.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the fs/Store wrapper:\n- Delegates to the wrapped ReadOnlyStore implementation\n- Uses the viewer pattern to ensure proper isolation\n- Returns the result from the underlying store\n\n```go\nfunc (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (exists bool, err error) {\n    return exists, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {\n        exists, err = ss.FlagExists(ctx, req)\n        return err\n    })\n}\n```\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Return Type**: `(bool, error)` instead of just `bool`\n   - Allows proper error handling for storage layer failures (e.g., database connection errors)\n   - Distinguishes between \"flag not found\" and \"error during lookup\"\n\n2. **SQL Implementation Strategy**: Using `COUNT(*) > 0` rather than fetching the flag\n   - More efficient as it only checks for existence without retrieving full flag data\n   - Indexes on (namespace_key, key) will make this query very fast\n\n3. **Snapshot Error Handling**: Returns `(false, nil)` when namespace doesn't exist\n   - Treats \"namespace not found\" as \"flag not found\" implicitly\n   - Keeps the implementation simple and focused\n\n4. **Cache Store**: Inherits implementation from embedded storage.Store\n   - Cache store embeds the underlying Store interface\n   - No separate implementation needed\n\n## Testing Considerations\n\nThe implementation should be tested with:\n1. **SQL Store**:\n   - Flag exists in default and custom namespaces\n   - Flag doesn't exist\n   - Namespace doesn't exist\n   - Database errors\n\n2. **Snapshot**:\n   - Flag exists in default and custom namespaces\n   - Flag doesn't exist\n   - Namespace doesn't exist\n\n3. **fs/Store**:\n   - All scenarios above through the wrapper\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\nAll existing code that uses `GetFlag()` continues to work as before. The new `FlagExists()` method is purely additive and provides a more efficient alternative for existence checks.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":314,"cache_read_input_tokens":118872,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":314},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5dad40b1-d53f-4b64-8b9e-ba98e6f9f0fd","uuid":"7aef9221-69c0-4d66-855e-19f64e202d48"}

Interface Definition\n**File:** `internal/storage/storage.go`\n\nUpdated the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface to include:\n```go\nFlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)\n```\n\nThis method provides a lightweight way to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object.\n\n### 2. SQL Store Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/sql/common/flag.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the SQL Store:\n- Uses a SQL query with `COUNT(*) > 0` to efficiently check existence\n- Respects the namespace and key from the ResourceRequest\n- Returns `(true, nil)` if the flag exists, `(false, nil)` otherwise\n- Returns `(false, err)` on database errors\n\n```go\nfunc (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {\n    var exists bool\n    err := s.builder.Select(\"COUNT(*) > 0\").\n        From(\"flags\").\n        Where(sq.Eq{\"namespace_key\": p.Namespace(), \"\\\"key\\\"\": p.Key}).\n        QueryRowContext(ctx).\n        Scan(&exists)\n    if err != nil {\n        return false, err\n    }\n    return exists, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Filesystem Snapshot Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/fs/snapshot_flag_exists.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the Snapshot type:\n- Checks if the flag exists in the in-memory namespace map\n- Returns `(false, nil)` if the namespace doesn't exist (not an error)\n- Returns `(true, nil)` if the flag exists in the namespace\n- Returns `(false, nil)` if the flag doesn't exist\n\n```go\nfunc (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {\n    ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())\n    if err != nil {\n        return false, nil\n    }\n    _, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]\n    return ok, nil\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Filesystem Store Wrapper Implementation\n**File:** `internal/storage/fs/store_flag_exists.go`\n\nImplemented `FlagExists` method for the fs/Store wrapper:\n- Delegates to the wrapped ReadOnlyStore implementation\n- Uses the viewer pattern to ensure proper isolation\n- Returns the result from the underlying store\n\n```go\nfunc (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (exists bool, err error) {\n    return exists, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {\n        exists, err = ss.FlagExists(ctx, req)\n        return err\n    })\n}\n```\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Return Type**: `(bool, error)` instead of just `bool`\n   - Allows proper error handling for storage layer failures (e.g., database connection errors)\n   - Distinguishes between \"flag not found\" and \"error during lookup\"\n\n2. **SQL Implementation Strategy**: Using `COUNT(*) > 0` rather than fetching the flag\n   - More efficient as it only checks for existence without retrieving full flag data\n   - Indexes on (namespace_key, key) will make this query very fast\n\n3. **Snapshot Error Handling**: Returns `(false, nil)` when namespace doesn't exist\n   - Treats \"namespace not found\" as \"flag not found\" implicitly\n   - Keeps the implementation simple and focused\n\n4. **Cache Store**: Inherits implementation from embedded storage.Store\n   - Cache store embeds the underlying Store interface\n   - No separate implementation needed\n\n## Testing Considerations\n\nThe implementation should be tested with:\n1. **SQL Store**:\n   - Flag exists in default and custom namespaces\n   - Flag doesn't exist\n   - Namespace doesn't exist\n   - Database errors\n\n2. **Snapshot**:\n   - Flag exists in default and custom namespaces\n   - Flag doesn't exist\n   - Namespace doesn't exist\n\n3. **fs/Store**:\n   - All scenarios above through the wrapper\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\nAll existing code that uses `GetFlag()` continues to work as before.
